      <p><b>Bahrain</b> (<span class="rt-commentedText nowrap"><span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">/<span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="'b' in 'buy'">b</span><span title="/ɑː/: 'a' in 'father'">ɑː</span><span title="/ˈ/: primary stress follows">ˈ</span><span title="'r' in 'rye'">r</span><span title="/eɪ/: 'a' in 'face'">eɪ</span><span title="'n' in 'nigh'">n</span></span>/</a></span> <span class="nowrap" style="font-size:85%">(<span class="unicode haudio"><span class="fn"><span style="white-space:nowrap;margin-right:.25em;"><a href="/wiki/File:En-us-Bahrain.ogg" title="About this sound"><img alt="About this sound" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/11px-Loudspeaker.svg.png" decoding="async" width="11" height="11" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/17px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/22px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="20" data-file-height="20"></a></span><a href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/c/cb/En-us-Bahrain.ogg" class="internal" title="En-us-Bahrain.ogg">listen</a></span></span>)</span></span> <a href="/wiki/Help:Pronunciation_respelling_key" title="Help:Pronunciation respelling key"><i title="English pronunciation respelling">bar-<span style="font-size:90%">AYN</span></i></a>; <a href="/wiki/Arabic_language" class="mw-redirect" title="Arabic language">Arabic</a>: <span lang="ar" dir="rtl">البحرين</span>‎, <small><a href="/wiki/Romanization_of_Arabic" title="Romanization of Arabic">romanized</a>:&nbsp;</small><i lang="ar-Latn" title="Arabic-language romanization">al-Baḥrayn</i>, <small>IPA:&nbsp;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Arabic" title="Help:IPA/Arabic">[al baħˈrajn]</a></span>, <small>locally</small> <small></small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Arabic" title="Help:IPA/Arabic">[æl baħˈreːn]</a></span> <span class="nowrap" style="font-size:85%">(<span class="unicode haudio"><span class="fn"><span style="white-space:nowrap;margin-right:.25em;"><a href="/wiki/File:Ar-Bahrain-1.oga" title="About this sound"><img alt="About this sound" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/11px-Loudspeaker.svg.png" decoding="async" width="11" height="11" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/17px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/22px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="20" data-file-height="20"></a></span><a href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/8/80/Ar-Bahrain-1.oga" class="internal" title="Ar-Bahrain-1.oga">listen</a></span></span>)</span>), officially the <b>Kingdom of Bahrain</b> (Arabic: <span lang="ar" dir="rtl">مملكة البحرين</span>‎ <i><span class="unicode haudio"><span class="fn"><span style="white-space:nowrap;margin-right:.25em;"><a href="/wiki/File:Ar-Mamlakat_al-Ba%E1%B8%A5rayn.oga" title="About this sound"><img alt="About this sound" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/11px-Loudspeaker.svg.png" decoding="async" width="11" height="11" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/17px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/22px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="20" data-file-height="20"></a></span><a href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/bb/Ar-Mamlakat_al-Ba%E1%B8%A5rayn.oga" class="internal" title="Ar-Mamlakat al-Baḥrayn.oga">Mamlakat al-Baḥrayn</a></span></span></i>), is a country in the <a href="/wiki/Persian_Gulf" title="Persian Gulf">Persian Gulf</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Island_country" title="Island country">island nation</a> comprises a small <a href="/wiki/Archipelago" title="Archipelago">archipelago</a> made up of 51 natural islands and an additional 33 <a href="/wiki/Artificial_island" title="Artificial island">artificial islands</a>, centered around <a href="/wiki/Bahrain_Island" title="Bahrain Island">Bahrain Island</a> which make up around 83 percent of the country's landmass. The country is situated between the <a href="/wiki/Qatar" title="Qatar">Qatari</a> peninsula and the north eastern coast of <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a> to which it is connected by the 25-kilometre (16&nbsp;mi) <a href="/wiki/King_Fahd_Causeway" title="King Fahd Causeway">King Fahd Causeway</a>. According to the 2010 census, Bahrain 2020 population is estimated at 1,701,575 people mid year according to UN data. Half of people counted are non-nationals willing to report their status.<sup id="cite_ref-2010-census_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2010-census-12">[12]</a></sup> At 780 square kilometres (300&nbsp;sq&nbsp;mi) in size, it is the <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_and_dependencies_by_area" title="List of countries and dependencies by area">third-smallest nation</a> in Asia after the <a href="/wiki/Maldives" title="Maldives">Maldives</a> and <a href="/wiki/Singapore" title="Singapore">Singapore</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup> The capital and largest city is <a href="/wiki/Manama" title="Manama">Manama</a>. </p>
      <p>Bahrain is the site of the ancient <a href="/wiki/Dilmun_civilization" class="mw-redirect" title="Dilmun civilization">Dilmun civilization</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-:1_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-14">[14]</a></sup> It has been famed since antiquity for its <a href="/wiki/Pearl_fisheries" class="mw-redirect" title="Pearl fisheries">pearl fisheries</a>, which were considered the best in the world into the 19th century.<sup id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTE''EB''1878_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTE''EB''1878-15">[15]</a></sup> Bahrain was one of the earliest areas to convert to <a href="/wiki/Islam" title="Islam">Islam</a>, during the lifetime of the <a href="/wiki/Prophet_Muhammad" class="mw-redirect" title="Prophet Muhammad">Prophet Muhammad</a> in 628 CE. Following a period of Arab rule, Bahrain was ruled by the <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_Empire" title="Portuguese Empire">Portuguese Empire</a> from 1521 until 1602, following the conquest by <a href="/wiki/Shah" title="Shah">Shah</a> <a href="/wiki/Abbas_I_of_Persia" class="mw-redirect" title="Abbas I of Persia">Abbas I</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Safavid_dynasty" title="Safavid dynasty">Safavid dynasty</a> under the <a href="/wiki/Persian_Empire" class="mw-redirect" title="Persian Empire">Persian Empire</a>. In 1783, the <a href="/wiki/Bani_Utbah" title="Bani Utbah">Bani Utbah</a> clan captured Bahrain from <a href="/wiki/Nasr_Al-Madhkur" title="Nasr Al-Madhkur">Nasr Al-Madhkur</a> and it has since been ruled by the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Khalifa" title="House of Khalifa">Al Khalifa royal family</a>, with <a href="/wiki/Ahmed_ibn_Muhammad_ibn_Khalifa" title="Ahmed ibn Muhammad ibn Khalifa">Ahmed al Fateh</a> as Bahrain's first <a href="/wiki/Hakim_(title)#In_Arab_countries" title="Hakim (title)"><i>hakim</i></a>. </p>
      <p>In the late 1800s, following successive treaties with the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_of_Great_Britain_and_Ireland" title="United Kingdom of Great Britain and Ireland">British</a>, Bahrain became a <a href="/wiki/Protectorate" title="Protectorate">protectorate</a> of the United Kingdom. In 1971, it <a href="/wiki/Independence_Day_(Bahrain)" title="Independence Day (Bahrain)">declared independence</a>. Formerly an <a href="/wiki/Emirate" title="Emirate">emirate</a>, Bahrain was declared an Islamic <a href="/wiki/Constitutional_monarchy" title="Constitutional monarchy">constitutional monarchy</a> in 2002. </p>
      <p>In 2011, the country experienced <a href="/wiki/Bahraini_uprising_of_2011" title="Bahraini uprising of 2011">protests</a> inspired by the regional <a href="/wiki/Arab_Spring" title="Arab Spring">Arab Spring</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup> Bahrain's ruling al-Khalifa royal family has been criticized for <a href="/wiki/Human_rights_in_Bahrain" title="Human rights in Bahrain">violating the human rights</a> of groups including dissidents, political opposition figures, and its majority <a href="/wiki/Shia_in_Bahrain" title="Shia in Bahrain">Shia Muslim population</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>Bahrain developed the first post-oil economy in the Persian Gulf,<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup> the result of decades of investing in the <a href="/wiki/Banking" class="mw-redirect" title="Banking">banking</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tourism" title="Tourism">tourism</a> sectors;<sup id="cite_ref-EDB_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EDB-19">[19]</a></sup> many of the world's largest financial institutions have a presence in the country's capital. It subsequently has a high <a href="/wiki/Human_Development_Index" title="Human Development Index">Human Development Index</a> and is recognised by the <a href="/wiki/World_Bank" title="World Bank">World Bank</a> as a <a href="/wiki/World_Bank_high-income_economy" title="World Bank high-income economy">high-income economy</a>. Bahrain is a member of the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a>, <a href="/wiki/Non-Aligned_Movement" title="Non-Aligned Movement">Non-Aligned Movement</a>, <a href="/wiki/Arab_League" title="Arab League">Arab League</a>, <a href="/wiki/Organisation_of_Islamic_Cooperation" title="Organisation of Islamic Cooperation">Organisation of Islamic Cooperation</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Gulf_Cooperation_Council" title="Gulf Cooperation Council">Gulf Cooperation Council</a>. </p>
      <p><span class="anchor" id="Etymology"></span><span class="anchor" id="Toponym"></span> </p>

          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-32"><a href="#Languages"><span class="tocnumber">7.3</span> <span class="toctext">Languages</span></a></li> 
          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-33"><a href="#Education"><span class="tocnumber">7.4</span> <span class="toctext">Education</span></a></li> 
          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-34"><a href="#Health"><span class="tocnumber">7.5</span> <span class="toctext">Health</span></a></li> 
         </ul> </li> 
        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-35"><a href="#Culture"><span class="tocnumber">8</span> <span class="toctext">Culture</span></a> 
         <ul> 
          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-36"><a href="#Art"><span class="tocnumber">8.1</span> <span class="toctext">Art</span></a></li>
